[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m139[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m140[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!d || !d->methods.get_description[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return NULL;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m141[0m[39m:    [0m[39mreturn d->methods.get_description [0m[1;39m([0m[39md, n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m142[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m143[0m[39m:    [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m144:c[0m[39mhar *[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m145:e[0m[39mxif_mnote_data_get_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *d, unsigned int n, char *val, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned int maxlen[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m146[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m147[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!d || !d->methods.get_value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return NULL;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m148[0m[39m:    [0m[39mreturn d->methods.get_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39md, n, val, maxlen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m149[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m150[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m151[0m[39m:void[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m152:e[0m[39mxif_mnote_data_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *d, ExifLog *log[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m153[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m154[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:    [0m[39mexif_log_unref [0m[1;39m([0m[39md->log[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m156[0m[39m:    [0m[39md->log = log;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m157[0m[39m:    [0m[39mexif_log_ref [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlog[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer report shows that in `exif_mnote_data_apple_load` the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode performs a `memcpy` of [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes into a buffer allocated for only [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m bytes.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The downstream copy logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_loader_copy`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m correctly respects the `size` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgiven to the loader, but the Apple-specific maker-note loader computes that `size` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtoo small by one byte [0m[1;39m([0m[39moff-by-one[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing the overflow when copying the full [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note content.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Code Flow:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `exif_data_load_data → interpret_maker_note → exif_mnote_data_load`  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → Apple loader’s `.load` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_load`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → calls into `exif_loader_write` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `exif_loader_copy` with `eld->size` bytes.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mexif_loader_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39ml, eld->size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` allocates exactly `eld->size` bytes.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apple loader computes and sets `eld->size` one byte less than the actual data [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength it later copies.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Approach:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Inspect `exif-mnote-data-apple.c` in `exif_mnote_data_apple_load`:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate the code that reads the maker-note length [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `maker_note_size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand then sets `eld->size` or invokes `exif_loader_write` with a derived size.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Likely there is a subtraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `maker_note_size - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to account for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msome header byte, but the subsequent `memcpy` still copies the full block including[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat byte.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Adjust Size Calculation:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure that the size passed to `exif_loader_write` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor assigned to [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`eld->size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m exactly matches the number of bytes that will be `memcpy`-ed.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If the current code does `size = raw_length – header_length - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, change it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `size = raw_length – header_length` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mremove the extra [0m[32m'-1'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, or if there is no [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader-length accounted, add [0m[32m'+1'[0m[39m to `eld->size`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Add Defensive Check:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before the `memcpy` in `exif_mnote_data_apple_load`, add a sanity check:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata_len > eld->size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Log truncated note rather than overflow *[0m[35m/[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Apple maker-note too large: truncating"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            data_len = eld->size;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This guarantees no overflow even under malformed maker-note lengths.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Preserve Behavior:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The patch only adjusts the computed `size` for Apple maker-note handling; [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit does not modify the generic loader, fuzz harness, or test code.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Existing tests and other maker-note implementations remain unaffected, as [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthey have independent size calculations.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Steps to Implement:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `libexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c`.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate `void [0m[1;35mexif_mnote_data_apple_load[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *d, const unsigned char[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*buf, unsigned int buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` around line [0m[1;36m131[0m[39m.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Identify the variable, say, `hdr_size` or `maker_size` that is assigned to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`eld->size` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthrough `exif_loader_copy`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or used directly in `memcpy`.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Remove the unintended `[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor equivalent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that under-allocates by one byte. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTypically change:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      maker_size = raw_size - [0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_LEN - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      maker_size = raw_size - [0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_LEN;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Immediately before the `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdest, buf+offset, maker_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, insert:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaker_size > buf_size - offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          maker_size = buf_size - offset;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      so that it never copies beyond the actual data.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun `exif_loader_fuzzer` to confirm the heap-buffer-overflow is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved and no new sanitizer errors appear.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Correcting the size calculation restores proper buffer bounds alignment and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevents the off-by-one overflow.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The defensive check guards against malformed inputs supplying inconsistent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlengths.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external APIs, fuzz harness, or test files are modified; only the Apple [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note loader logic is updated.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar patterns appear in other maker-note loaders [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., Fuji, Nikon[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize calculations precisely match copied bytes. We mirror their safe approach.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If other logic expects the original [0m[1;39m([0m[39munder-sized[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m buffer, ensure no downstream[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode relies on that one-byte truncation.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: run the full test suite [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding maker-note decoding [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregressions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to validate no functional change.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The added check logs truncation but does not abort; in the rare case of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed tags, the loader will still return best-effort data without overflowing.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Conclusion:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This targeted fix addresses the specific overflow in Apple maker-note parsing,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maligns allocated buffer size with actual copy length, and maintains existing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and tests.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify and isolate the vulnerable block in `exif_mnote_data_apple_load`:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate the loop over entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround source lines [0m[1;36m109[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m133[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Focus on the two lines that unconditionally perform `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, dsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.size = dsize;`.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Remove the original unconditional copy and size assignment:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete line containing `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39md->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.data, buf + dofs, dsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete line containing `d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.size = dsize;`.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Insert a single guarded copy sequence immediately after the allocation‐failure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Compute the number of bytes actually available in the buffer:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      unsigned int avail = buf_size > dofs ? buf_size - dofs : [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Determine how many bytes we will copy—either the full `dsize` or the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncated `avail`:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      unsigned int copy_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdsize < avail[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? dsize : avail;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Perform a bounded memcpy using `copy_len`:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39md->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.data, buf + dofs, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Record the actual number of bytes copied:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.size = copy_len;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Ensure brace and indentation integrity:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not introduce any extra `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` beyond the single-block structure of the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor‐loop.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The for‐loop should remain:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < tcount; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         … allocation …[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mEXIF_LOG_NO_MEMORY[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             continue;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* New guarded copy goes here, no additional braces *[0m[35m/[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         unsigned int avail = …;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         unsigned int copy_len = …;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39m… copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.size = copy_len;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     d->count = tcount;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     return;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After patching, compile and verify that there are no “function definition is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot allowed here” or “expected ‘[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m’” errors, confirming braces are balanced.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preserve existing behavior:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Skip entries on allocation failure [0m[1;39m([0m[39munchanged[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not skip or remove tags on truncated reads—only copy as much data as [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavailable.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep logging macros [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`EXIF_LOG_NO_MEMORY`, `exif_log`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unchanged to maintain [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdiagnostic output.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validate the patch:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild the library; ensure no compile errors.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun `exif_loader_fuzzer`; confirm that the heap‐buffer‐overflow no longer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the existing test suite to verify no regressions.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhy this approach works:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It directly addresses the root cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreading more bytes than available[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It avoids any brace‐mismatch by inserting only straight‐line code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno extra [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblocks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It maintains the function boundary integrity so subsequent static functions are [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly parsed.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It preserves all logging and error‐handling logic.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It is analogous to the existing overflow checks in `exif-mnote-data-fuji.c` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout altering the fuzzing harness or external utility functions.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
